<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "I'll implement **Task 10: Distributed transaction coordinator** - two-phase commit for cross-shard transactions.\n\n<WriteFile>\n<fileName>distributed_tx.py</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nDistributed Transaction Coordinator for KosDB\n\nImplements two-phase commit (2PC) protocol for cross-shard transactions.\nEnsures atomicity across multiple database shards.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport time\nimport uuid\nimport json\nimport threading\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Callable, Set, Tuple\nfrom enum import Enum, auto\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\n\nclass TransactionState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"States of a distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    ACTIVE = auto()         # Transaction started\n    PREPARING = auto()      # Phase 1: sending prepare\n    PREPARED = auto()       # Phase 1: all participants prepared\n    COMMITTING = auto()     # Phase 2: sending commit\n    COMMITTED = auto()      # Phase 2: all participants committed\n    ABORTING = auto()       # Phase 2: sending abort\n    ABORTED = auto()        # Phase 2: all participants aborted\n    HEURISTIC_ABORT = auto()  # Uncertain state, aborted heuristically\n\n\nclass ParticipantState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"States of a participant in distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    ACTIVE = auto()         # Transaction active on participant\n    PREPARED = auto()       # Participant prepared to commit\n    COMMITTED = auto()      # Participant committed\n    ABORTED = auto()        # Participant aborted\n    FAILED = auto()         # Participant failed\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Participant:\n    \"\"\"Participant in distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    participant_id: str\n    shard_id: str\n    connection: Any  # Connection to shard\n    state: ParticipantState = ParticipantState.ACTIVE\n    vote: Optional[bool] = None  # True=commit, False=abort, None=not voted\n    last_contact: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    \n    def touch(self):\n        \"\"\"Update last contact time.\"\"\"\n        self.last_contact = time.time()\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DistributedTransaction:\n    \"\"\"\n    Represents a distributed transaction.\n    \"\"\"\n    txn_id: str\n    coordinator_id: str\n    state: TransactionState = TransactionState.ACTIVE\n    participants: Dict[str, Participant] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    start_time: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    commit_time: Optional[float] = None\n    abort_reason: Optional[str] = None\n    decision: Optional[bool] = None  # Final decision (True=commit, False=abort)\n    \n    def add_participant(self, participant: Participant):\n        \"\"\"Add participant to transaction.\"\"\"\n        self.participants[participant.participant_id] = participant\n    \n    def all_prepared(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if all participants are prepared.\"\"\"\n        return all(\n            p.state == ParticipantState.PREPARED and p.vote is True\n            for p in self.participants.values()\n        )\n    \n    def any_aborted(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if any participant voted to abort.\"\"\"\n        return any(\n            p.vote is False or p.state == ParticipantState.ABORTED\n            for p in self.participants.values()\n        )\n    \n    def get_state_summary(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get transaction state summary.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            'txn_id': self.txn_id,\n            'coordinator': self.coordinator_id,\n            'state': self.state.name,\n            'participants': len(self.participants),\n            'prepared': sum(1 for p in self.participants.values() \n                          if p.state == ParticipantState.PREPARED),\n            'duration': time.time() - self.start_time\n        }\n\n\nclass TwoPhaseCommitCoordinator:\n    \"\"\"\n    Coordinator for two-phase commit protocol.\nn    Manages distributed transactions across multiple shards.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, coordinator_id: str, timeout: float = 30.0):\n        self.coordinator_id = coordinator_id\n        self.timeout = timeout\n        \n        self._transactions: Dict[str, DistributedTransaction] = {}\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n        self._running = False\n        self._cleanup_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None\n        \n        # Callbacks for participant communication\n        self._prepare_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._commit_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._abort_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self._running = True\n        self._cleanup_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._cleanup_loop)\n        self._cleanup_thread.daemon = True\n        self._cleanup_thread.start()\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self._running = False\n        if self._cleanup_thread:\n            self._cleanup_thread.join(timeout=5.0)\n    \n    def _cleanup_loop(self):\n        \"\"\"Background cleanup of expired transactions.\"\"\"\n        while self._running:\n            time.sleep(10.0)\n            self._cleanup_expired()\n    \n    def _cleanup_expired(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up expired transactions.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\nn            now = time.time()\\n            expired = [\\n                txn_id for txn_id, txn in self._transactions.items()\\n                if now - txn.start_time > self.timeout * 2\\n                and txn.state in (TransactionState.COMMITTED, \\n                                  TransactionState.ABORTED,\\n                                  TransactionState.HEURISTIC_ABORT)\\n            ]\\n            for txn_id in expired:\\n                del self._transactions[txn_id]\n    \n    def begin_transaction(self, participant_shards: List[Tuple[str, Any]]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Begin new distributed transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            participant_shards: List of (shard_id, connection) tuples\n        \n        Returns:\n            Transaction ID\n        \"\"\"\nn        txn_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\\n        \\n        txn = DistributedTransaction(\\n            txn_id=txn_id,\\n            coordinator_id=self.coordinator_id\\n        )\\n        \\n        for shard_id, connection in participant_shards:\\n            participant = Participant(\\n                participant_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),\\n                shard_id=shard_id,\\n                connection=connection\\n            )\\n            txn.add_participant(participant)\\n        \\n        with self._lock:\\n            self._transactions[txn_id] = txn\\n        \\n        print(f\"[2PC] Started transaction {txn_id} with {len(participant_shards)} participants\")\\n        return txn_id\n    \n    def prepare_phase(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Phase 1: Prepare all participants.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if all participants prepared successfully\n        \"\"\"\nn        with self._lock:\\n            txn = self._transactions.get(txn_id)\\n            if not txn:\\n                raise ValueError(f\"Unknown transaction: {txn_id}\")\n            \n            if txn.state != TransactionState.ACTIVE:\nn                raise ValueError(f\"Invalid transaction state: {txn.state}\")\\n            \\n            txn.state = TransactionState.PREPARING\\n        \\n        print(f\"[2PC] Starting prepare phase for {txn_id}\")\n        \n        # Ask each participant to prepare\n        all_prepared = True\n        for participant in txn.participants.values():\n            try:\n                prepared = self._send_prepare(participant, txn_id)\n                participant.vote = prepared\n                participant.state = (ParticipantState.PREPARED \n                                   if prepared else ParticipantState.ABORTED)\nn                participant.touch()\\n                \\n                if not prepared:\\n                    all_prepared = False\\n                    txn.abort_reason = f\"Participant {participant.shard_id} voted no\"\nn                    break\\n            except Exception as e:\\n                participant.state = ParticipantState.FAILED\\n                all_prepared = False\\n                txn.abort_reason = f\"Participant {participant.shard_id} failed: {e}\"\nn                break\\n        \\n        with self._lock:\\n            if all_prepared:\\n                txn.state = TransactionState.PREPARED\\n                txn.decision = True\\n                print(f\"[2PC] All participants prepared for {txn_id}\")\nn                return True\\n            else:\\n                txn.state = TransactionState.ABORTING\\n                txn.decision = False\\n                print(f\"[2PC] Prepare failed for {txn_id}: {txn.abort_reason}\")\nn                return False\\n    \\n    def commit_phase(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Phase 2: Commit transaction.\n        \n        Args:\nn            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if commit successful\n        \"\"\"\nn        with self._lock:\\n            txn = self._transactions.get(txn_id)\\n            if not txn:\\n                raise ValueError(f\"Unknown transaction: {txn_id}\")\n            \nn            if txn.state != TransactionState.PREPARED:\\n                raise ValueError(f\"Transaction not prepared: {txn.state}\")\n            \n            txn.state = TransactionState.COMMITTING\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Starting commit phase for {txn_id}\")\n        \n        # Send commit to all participants\n        committed = []\n        failed = []\n        \n        for participant in txn.participants.values():\n            try:\n                self._send_commit(participant, txn_id)\n                participant.state = ParticipantState.COMMITTED\n                participant.touch()\n                committed.append(participant.participant_id)\n            except Exception as e:\n                failed.append((participant.participant_id, str(e)))\n        \n        with self._lock:\nn            if not failed:\\n                txn.state = TransactionState.COMMITTED\\n                txn.commit_time = time.time()\\n                print(f\"[2PC] Transaction {txn_id} committed successfully\")\\n                return True\\n            else:\\n                # Some participants failed - transaction uncertain\\n                print(f\"[2PC] Warning: {len(failed)} participants failed to commit {txn_id}\")\nn                return False\\n    \\n    def abort_transaction(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Abort distributed transaction.\n        \n        Args:\nn            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if abort successful\n        \"\"\"\nn        with self._lock:\\n            txn = self._transactions.get(txn_id)\\n            if not txn:\\n                return False\n            \n            if txn.state in (TransactionState.COMMITTED, TransactionState.ABORTED):\\n                return True  # Already terminal\\n            \\n            txn.state = TransactionState.ABORTING\\n            txn.decision = False\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Aborting transaction {txn_id}\")\n        \n        # Send abort to all participants\n        for participant in txn.participants.values():\n            try:\n                if participant.state not in (ParticipantState.COMMITTED, \nn                                            ParticipantState.ABORTED):\\n                    self._send_abort(participant, txn_id)\\n                    participant.state = ParticipantState.ABORTED\\n                    participant.touch()\\n            except Exception as e:\\n                print(f\"[2PC] Warning: failed to abort participant {participant.shard_id}: {e}\")\nn        \\n        with self._lock:\\n            txn.state = TransactionState.ABORTED\\n        \\n        return True\n    \n    def execute_transaction(self, txn_id: str, \n                           operations: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute full 2PC transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n            operations: List of operations to execute\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if transaction committed\n        \"\"\"\n        # Phase 1: Prepare\n        if not self.prepare_phase(txn_id):\nn            # Prepare failed, abort\\n            self.abort_transaction(txn_id)\\n            return False\n        \n        # Phase 2: Commit\n        return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\n    \n    def _send_prepare(self, participant: Participant, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Send prepare request to participant.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        if self._prepare_callback:\\n            return self._prepare_callback(participant, txn_id)\n        \\n        # Default: simulate prepare\\n        print(f\"[2PC] Sending PREPARE to {participant.shard_id}\")\nn        time.sleep(0.001)  # Simulate network\\n        return True\n    \n    def _send_commit(self, participant: Participant, txn_id: str):\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Send commit to participant.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        if self._commit_callback:\\n            self._commit_callback(participant, txn_id)\nn        else:\\n            print(f\"[2PC] Sending COMMIT to {participant.shard_id}\")\nn            time.sleep(0.001)  # Simulate network\\n    \\n    def _send_abort(self, participant: Participant, txn_id: str):\nn        \\\"\\\"\\\"Send abort to participant.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        if self._abort_callback:\\n            self._abort_callback(participant, txn_id)\\n        else:\\n            print(f\"[2PC] Sending ABORT to {participant.shard_id}\")\nn            time.sleep(0.001)  # Simulate network\\n    \\n    def get_transaction(self, txn_id: str) -> Optional[DistributedTransaction]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Get transaction by ID.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        with self._lock:\\n            return self._transactions.get(txn_id)\\n    \\n    def get_active_transactions(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Get list of active transactions.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        with self._lock:\\n            return [\\n                txn.get_state_summary()\\n                for txn in self._transactions.values()\\n                if txn.state not in (TransactionState.COMMITTED,\\n                                     TransactionState.ABORTED)\\n            ]\\n    \\n    def recover_transaction(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Recover transaction after coordinator failure.\n        \n        Args:\\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if recovery successful\n        \"\"\"\nn        txn = self.get_transaction(txn_id)\\n        if not txn:\\n            return False\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Recovering transaction {txn_id} in state {txn.state.name}\")\n        \n        if txn.state == TransactionState.PREPARED:\\n            # We decided to commit but may not have notified all\\n            return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\\n        elif txn.state == TransactionState.COMMITTING:\\n            # Commit in progress, retry\\n            return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\\n        elif txn.state == TransactionState.ABORTING:\\n            # Abort in progress, retry\\n            return self.abort_transaction(txn_id)\\n        else:\\n            print(f\"[2PC] Transaction {txn_id} in state {txn.state.name}, no recovery needed\")\nn            return True\\n\\n\\nclass ShardParticipant:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Participant side of 2PC protocol.\\n    Runs on each shard to handle coordinator requests.\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    \\n    def __init__(self, shard_id: str, db: Any):\\n        self.shard_id = shard_id\\n        self.db = db\\n        self._prepared_txns: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}  # txn_id -> saved state\\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\\n    \\n    def prepare(self, txn_id: str, operations: List[Dict]) -> bool:\nn        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Prepare to commit transaction.\\n        \\n        Args:\nn            txn_id: Transaction ID\\n            operations: Operations to execute\\n        \\n        Returns:\\n            True if prepared successfully\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Preparing transaction {txn_id}\")\nn        \\n        try:\\n            # Validate operations can be executed\\n            for op in operations:\\n                if not self._validate_operation(op):\\n                    return False\n            \n            # Save state for potential commit/abort\\n            with self._lock:\\n                self._prepared_txns[txn_id] = {\\n                    'operations': operations,\\n                    'prepared_at': time.time(),\\n                    'state': 'prepared'\\n                }\n            \nn            return True\\n        except Exception as e:\\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Prepare failed: {e}\")\nn            return False\\n    \\n    def commit(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Commit prepared transaction.\n        \n        Args:\nn            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if committed successfully\n        \"\"\"\nn        with self._lock:\\n            txn = self._prepared_txns.get(txn_id)\\n            if not txn:\\n                # Already committed or unknown\\n                return True\n            \nn            if txn['state'] != 'prepared':\\n                return False\n            \nn            try:\\n                # Execute operations\\n                for op in txn['operations']:\\n                    self._execute_operation(op)\\n                \\n                txn['state'] = 'committed'\\n                print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Committed transaction {txn_id}\")\nn                return True\\n            except Exception as e:\\n                print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Commit failed: {e}\")\nn                return False\\n    \\n    def abort(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Abort prepared transaction.\n        \n        Args:\nn            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if aborted successfully\n        \"\"\"\nn        with self._lock:\\n            txn = self._prepared_txns.get(txn_id)\\n            if not txn:\\n                return True  # Already aborted or unknown\n            \nn            txn['state'] = 'aborted'\\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Aborted transaction {txn_id}\")\nn            return True\\n    \\n    def _validate_operation(self, op: Dict) -> bool:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Validate operation can be executed.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        # Check table exists, constraints, etc.\\n        return True\\n    \\n    def _execute_operation(self, op: Dict):\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Execute single operation.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        op_type = op.get('type')\\n        table = op.get('table')\\n        \\n        if op_type == 'insert':\\n            key = op['key']\\n            data = op['data']\\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] INSERT {table}.{key}\\\")\\n        elif op_type == 'update':\\n            key = op['key']\\n            data = op['data']\\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] UPDATE {table}.{key}\\\")\\n        elif op_type == 'delete':\\n            key = op['key']\\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] DELETE {table}.{key}\\\")\\n\\n\\nclass DistributedTransactionManager:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    High-level manager for distributed transactions.\nn    Combines coordinator and participant functionality.\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    \\n    def __init__(self, node_id: str, is_coordinator: bool = False):\\n        self.node_id = node_id\\n        self.is_coordinator = is_coordinator\\n        \\n        if is_coordinator:\\n            self.coordinator = TwoPhaseCommitCoordinator(node_id)\\n        else:\\n            self.coordinator = None\\n        \\n        self.participant: Optional[ShardParticipant] = None\\n        self._shards: Dict[str, Any] = {}  # shard_id -> connection\n    \n    def register_shard(self, shard_id: str, connection: Any):\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Register a shard connection.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        self._shards[shard_id] = connection\n    \n    def execute_cross_shard(self, operations_by_shard: Dict[str, List[Dict]]) -> str:\nn        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Execute operations across multiple shards.\n        \n        Args:\nn            operations_by_shard: Map of shard_id -> operations\\n        \\n        Returns:\nn            Transaction ID\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        if not self.is_coordinator:\\n            raise RuntimeError(\"Only coordinator can execute cross-shard transactions\")\nn        \\n        # Get participants\\n        participants = []\\n        for shard_id in operations_by_shard.keys():\\n            if shard_id not in self._shards:\\n                raise ValueError(f\"Unknown shard: {shard_id}\")\nn            participants.append((shard_id, self._shards[shard_id]))\nn        \\n        # \\n        return txn_id, success\n    \n    def get_transaction_status(self, txn_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\nn        \\\"\\\"\\\"Get transaction status.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        if not > Distributed Transaction Coordinator for KosDB
> 
> Implements two-phase commit (2PC) protocol for cross-shard transactions.
> Ensures atomicity across multiple database shards.

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>distributed_tx.py</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nDistributed Transaction Coordinator for KosDB\n\nImplements two-phase commit (2PC) protocol for cross-shard transactions.\nEnsures atomicity across multiple database shards.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport time\nimport uuid\nimport json\nimport threading\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Callable, Set, Tuple\nfrom enum import Enum, auto\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\n\nclass TransactionState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"States of a distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    ACTIVE = auto()         # Transaction started\n    PREPARING = auto()      # Phase 1: sending prepare\n    PREPARED = auto()       # Phase 1: all participants prepared\n    COMMITTING = auto()     # Phase 2: sending commit\n    COMMITTED = auto()      # Phase 2: all participants committed\n    ABORTING = auto()       # Phase 2: sending abort\n    ABORTED = auto()        # Phase 2: all participants aborted\n    HEURISTIC_ABORT = auto()  # Uncertain state, aborted heuristically\n\n\nclass ParticipantState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"States of a participant in distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    ACTIVE = auto()         # Transaction active on participant\n    PREPARED = auto()       # Participant prepared to commit\n    COMMITTED = auto()      # Participant committed\n    ABORTED = auto()        # Participant aborted\n    FAILED = auto()         # Participant failed\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Participant:\n    \"\"\"Participant in distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    participant_id: str\n    shard_id: str\n    connection: Any  # Connection to shard\n    state: ParticipantState = ParticipantState.ACTIVE\n    vote: Optional[bool] = None  # True=commit, False=abort, None=not voted\n    last_contact: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    \n    def touch(self):\n        \"\"\"Update last contact time.\"\"\"\n        self.last_contact = time.time()\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DistributedTransaction:\n    \"\"\"\n    Represents a distributed transaction.\n    \"\"\"\n    txn_id: str\n    coordinator_id: str\n    state: TransactionState = TransactionState.ACTIVE\n    participants: Dict[str, Participant] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    start_time: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    commit_time: Optional[float] = None\n    abort_reason: Optional[str] = None\n    decision: Optional[bool] = None  # Final decision (True=commit, False=abort)\n    \n    def add_participant(self, participant: Participant):\n        \"\"\"Add participant to transaction.\"\"\"\n        self.participants[participant.participant_id] = participant\n    \n    def all_prepared(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if all participants are prepared.\"\"\"\n        return all(\n            p.state == ParticipantState.PREPARED and p.vote is True\n            for p in self.participants.values()\n        )\n    \n    def any_aborted(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if any participant voted to abort.\"\"\"\n        return any(\n            p.vote is False or p.state == ParticipantState.ABORTED\n            for p in self.participants.values()\n        )\n    \n    def get_state_summary(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get transaction state summary.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            'txn_id': self.txn_id,\n            'coordinator': self.coordinator_id,\n            'state': self.state.name,\n            'participants': len(self.participants),\n            'prepared': sum(1 for p in self.participants.values() \n                          if p.state == ParticipantState.PREPARED),\n            'duration': time.time() - self.start_time\n        }\n\n\nclass TwoPhaseCommitCoordinator:\n    \"\"\"\n    Coordinator for two-phase commit protocol.\n    Manages distributed transactions across multiple shards.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, coordinator_id: str, timeout: float = 30.0):\n        self.coordinator_id = coordinator_id\n        self.timeout = timeout\n        \n        self._transactions: Dict[str, DistributedTransaction] = {}\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n        self._running = False\n        self._cleanup_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None\n        \n        # Callbacks for participant communication\n        self._prepare_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._commit_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._abort_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self._running = True\n        self._cleanup_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._cleanup_loop)\n        self._cleanup_thread.daemon = True\n        self._cleanup_thread.start()\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self._running = False\n        if self._cleanup_thread:\n            self._cleanup_thread.join(timeout=5.0)\n    \n    def _cleanup_loop(self):\n        \"\"\"Background cleanup of expired transactions.\"\"\"\n        while self._running:\n            time.sleep(10.0)\n            self._cleanup_expired()\n    \n    def _cleanup_expired(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up expired transactions.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            now = time.time()\n            expired = [\n                txn_id for txn_id, txn in self._transactions.items()\n                if now - txn.start_time > self.timeout * 2\n                and txn.state in (TransactionState.COMMITTED, \n                                  TransactionState.ABORTED,\n                                  TransactionState.HEURISTIC_ABORT)\n            ]\n            for txn_id in expired:\n                del self._transactions[txn_id]\n    \n    def begin_transaction(self, participant_shards: List[Tuple[str, Any]]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Begin new distributed transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            participant_shards: List of (shard_id, connection) tuples\n        \n        Returns:\n            Transaction ID\n        \"\"\"\n        txn_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        \n        txn = DistributedTransaction(\n            txn_id=txn_id,\n            coordinator_id=self.coordinator_id\n        )\n        \n        for shard_id, connection in participant_shards:\n            participant = Participant(\n                participant_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),\n                shard_id=shard_id,\n                connection=connection\n            )\n            txn.add_participant(participant)\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            self._transactions[txn_id] = txn\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Started transaction {txn_id} with {len(participant_shards)} participants\")\n        return txn_id\n    \n    def prepare_phase(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Phase 1: Prepare all participants.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if all participants prepared successfully\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            txn = self._transactions.get(txn_id)\n            if not txn:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Unknown transaction: {txn_id}\")\n            \n            if txn.state != TransactionState.ACTIVE:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Invalid transaction state: {txn.state}\")\n            \n            txn.state = TransactionState.PREPARING\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Starting prepare phase for {txn_id}\")\n        \n        # Ask each participant to prepare\n        all_prepared = True\n        for participant in txn.participants.values():\n            try:\n                prepared = self._send_prepare(participant, txn_id)\n                participant.vote = prepared\n                participant.state = (ParticipantState.PREPARED \n                                   if prepared else ParticipantState.ABORTED)\n                participant.touch()\n                \n                if not prepared:\n                    all_prepared = False\n                    txn.abort_reason = f\"Participant {participant.shard_id} voted no\"\n                    break\n            except Exception as e:\n                participant.state = ParticipantState.FAILED\n                all_prepared = False\n                txn.abort_reason = f\"Participant {participant.shard_id} failed: {e}\"\n                break\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            if all_prepared:\n                txn.state = TransactionState.PREPARED\n                txn.decision = True\n                print(f\"[2PC] All participants prepared for {txn_id}\")\n                return True\n            else:\n                txn.state = TransactionState.ABORTING\n                txn.decision = False\n                print(f\"[2PC] Prepare failed for {txn_id}: {txn.abort_reason}\")\n                return False\n    \n    def commit_phase(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Phase 2: Commit transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if commit successful\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            txn = self._transactions.get(txn_id)\n            if not txn:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Unknown transaction: {txn_id}\")\n            \n            if txn.state != TransactionState.PREPARED:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Transaction not prepared: {txn.state}\")\n            \n            txn.state = TransactionState.COMMITTING\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Starting commit phase for {txn_id}\")\n        \n        # Send commit to all participants\n        committed = []\n        failed = []\n        \n        for participant in txn.participants.values():\n            try:\n                self._send_commit(participant, txn_id)\n                participant.state = ParticipantState.COMMITTED\n                participant.touch()\n                committed.append(participant.participant_id)\n            except Exception as e:\n                failed.append((participant.participant_id, str(e)))\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            if not failed:\n                txn.state = TransactionState.COMMITTED\n                txn.commit_time = time.time()\n                print(f\"[2PC] Transaction {txn_id} committed successfully\")\n                return True\n            else:\n                # Some participants failed - transaction uncertain\n                print(f\"[2PC] Warning: {len(failed)} participants failed to commit {txn_id}\")\n                return False\n    \n    def abort_transaction(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Abort distributed transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if abort successful\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            txn = self._transactions.get(txn_id)\n            if not txn:\n                return False\n            \n            if txn.state in (TransactionState.COMMITTED, TransactionState.ABORTED):\n                return True  # Already terminal\n            \n            txn.state = TransactionState.ABORTING\n            txn.decision = False\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Aborting transaction {txn_id}\")\n        \n        # Send abort to all participants\n        for participant in txn.participants.values():\n            try:\n                if participant.state not in (ParticipantState.COMMITTED, \n                                            ParticipantState.ABORTED):\n                    self._send_abort(participant, txn_id)\n                    participant.state = ParticipantState.ABORTED\n                    participant.touch()\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[2PC] Warning: failed to abort participant {participant.shard_id}: {e}\")\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            txn.state = TransactionState.ABORTED\n        \n        return True\n    \n    def execute_transaction(self, txn_id: str, \n                           operations: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute full 2PC transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n            operations: List of operations to execute\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if transaction committed\n        \"\"\"\n        # Phase 1: Prepare\n        if not self.prepare_phase(txn_id):\n            # Prepare failed, abort\n            self.abort_transaction(txn_id)\n            return False\n        \n        # Phase 2: Commit\n        return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\n    \n    def _send_prepare(self, participant: Participant, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Send prepare request to participant.\"\"\"\n        if self._prepare_callback:\n            return self._prepare_callback(participant, txn_id)\n        \n        # Default: simulate prepare\n        print(f\"[2PC] Sending PREPARE to {participant.shard_id}\")\n        time.sleep(0.001)  # Simulate network\n        return True\n    \n    def _send_commit(self, participant: Participant, txn_id: str):\n        \"\"\"Send commit to participant.\"\"\"\n        if self._commit_callback:\n            self._commit_callback(participant, txn_id)\n        else:\n            print(f\"[2PC] Sending COMMIT to {participant.shard_id}\")\n            time.sleep(0.001)  # Simulate network\n    \n    def _send_abort(self, participant: Participant, txn_id: str):\n        \"\"\"Send abort to participant.\"\"\"\n        if self._abort_callback:\n            self._abort_callback(participant, txn_id)\n        else:\n            print(f\"[2PC] Sending ABORT to {participant.shard_id}\")\n            time.sleep(0.001)  # Simulate network\n    \n    def get_transaction(self, txn_id: str) -> Optional[DistributedTransaction]:\n        \"\"\"Get transaction by ID.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return self._transactions.get(txn_id)\n    \n    def get_active_transactions(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Get list of active transactions.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return [\n                txn.get_state_summary()\n                for txn in self._transactions.values()\n                if txn.state not in (TransactionState.COMMITTED,\n                                     TransactionState.ABORTED)\n            ]\n    \n    def recover_transaction(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Recover transaction after coordinator failure.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if recovery successful\n        \"\"\"\n        txn = self.get_transaction(txn_id)\n        if not txn:\n            return False\n        \n        print(f\"[2PC] Recovering transaction {txn_id} in state {txn.state.name}\")\n        \n        if txn.state == TransactionState.PREPARED:\n            # We decided to commit but may not have notified all\n            return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\n        elif txn.state == TransactionState.COMMITTING:\n            # Commit in progress, retry\n            return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\n        elif txn.state == TransactionState.ABORTING:\n            # Abort in progress, retry\n            return self.abort_transaction(txn_id)\n        else:\n            print(f\"[2PC] Transaction {txn_id} in state {txn.state.name}, no recovery needed\")\n            return True\n\n\nclass ShardParticipant:\n    \"\"\"\n    Participant side of 2PC protocol.\n    Runs on each shard to handle coordinator requests.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, shard_id: str, db: Any):\n        self.shard_id = shard_id\n        self.db = db\n        self._prepared_txns: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}  # txn_id -> saved state\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n    \n    def prepare(self, txn_id: str, operations: List[Dict]) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Prepare to commit transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n            operations: Operations to execute\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if prepared successfully\n        \"\"\"\n        print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Preparing transaction {txn_id}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Validate operations can be executed\n            for op in operations:\n                if not self._validate_operation(op):\n                    return False\n            \n            # Save state for potential commit/abort\n            with self._lock:\n                self._prepared_txns[txn_id] = {\n                    'operations': operations,\n                    'prepared_at': time.time(),\n                    'state': 'prepared'\n                }\n            \n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Prepare failed: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def commit(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Commit prepared transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if committed successfully\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            txn = self._prepared_txns.get(txn_id)\n            if not txn:\n                # Already committed or unknown\n                return True\n            \n            if txn['state'] != 'prepared':\n                return False\n            \n            try:\n                # Execute operations\n                for op in txn['operations']:\n                    self._execute_operation(op)\n                \n                txn['state'] = 'committed'\n                print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Committed transaction {txn_id}\")\n                return True\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Commit failed: {e}\")\n                return False\n    \n    def abort(self, txn_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Abort prepared transaction.\n        \n        Args:\n            txn_id: Transaction ID\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if aborted successfully\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            txn = self._prepared_txns.get(txn_id)\n            if not txn:\n                return True  # Already aborted or unknown\n            \n            txn['state'] = 'aborted'\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] Aborted transaction {txn_id}\")\n            return True\n    \n    def _validate_operation(self, op: Dict) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Validate operation can be executed.\"\"\"\n        # Check table exists, constraints, etc.\n        return True\n    \n    def _execute_operation(self, op: Dict):\n        \"\"\"Execute single operation.\"\"\"\n        op_type = op.get('type')\n        table = op.get('table')\n        \n        if op_type == 'insert':\n            key = op['key']\n            data = op['data']\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] INSERT {table}.{key}\")\n        elif op_type == 'update':\n            key = op['key']\n            data = op['data']\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] UPDATE {table}.{key}\")\n        elif op_type == 'delete':\n            key = op['key']\n            print(f\"[Shard {self.shard_id}] DELETE {table}.{key}\")\n\n\nclass DistributedTransactionManager:\n    \"\"\"\n    High-level manager for distributed transactions.\n    Combines coordinator and participant functionality.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, node_id: str, is_coordinator: bool = False):\n        self.node_id = node_id\n        self.is_coordinator = is_coordinator\n        \n        if is_coordinator:\n            self.coordinator = TwoPhaseCommitCoordinator(node_id)\n        else:\n            self.coordinator = None\n        \n        self.participant: <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>distributed_tx.py</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nDistributed Transaction Coordinator for KosDB\n\nImplements two-phase commit (2PC) protocol for cross-shard transactions.\nEnsures atomicity across multiple database shards.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport time\nimport uuid\nimport json\nimport threading\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, ACTIVE = auto()         # Transaction started\n    PREPARING = auto()      # Phase 1: sending prepare\n    PREPARED = auto()       # Phase 1: all participants prepared\n    COMMITTING = auto()     # Phase 2: sending commit\n    COMMITTED = auto()      # Phase 2: all participants committed\n    ABORTING = auto()       # Phase 2: sending abort\n    ABORTED = auto()        # Phase 2: all participants aborted\n    HEURISTIC_ABORT = auto()  # Uncertain state, aborted heuristically\n\n\nclass ParticipantState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"States of a participant in distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    ACTIVE = auto()         # Transaction active on participant\n    PREPARED = auto()       # Participant prepared to commit\n    COMMITTED = auto()      # Participant committed\n    ABORTED = auto()        # Participant aborted\n    FAILED = auto()         # Participant failed\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Participant:\n    \"\"\"Participant in distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    participant_id: str\n last_contact: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    \n    def touch(self):\n        \"\"\"Update last contact time.\"\"\"\n        self.last_contact = time.time()\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DistributedTransaction:\n    \"\"\"\n    Represents a distributed transaction.\n    \"\"\"\n    txn_id: str\n    coordinator_id: str\n    state: TransactionState = TransactionState.ACTIVE\n \"\"\"Check if any participant voted to abort.\"\"\"\n        return any(\n            p.vote is False or p.state == ParticipantState.ABORTED\n            for p in self.participants.values()\n        )\n    \n    def get_state_summary(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get transaction state summary.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            'txn_id': self.txn_id,\n            'coordinator':        if p.state == ParticipantState.PREPARED),\n            'duration': time.time() - self.start_time\n        }\n\n\nclass TwoPhaseCommitCoordinator:\n    \"\"\"\n    Coordinator for two-phase commit protocol.\n    Manages distributed transactions across multiple shards.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, coordinator_id: str, timeout: float = 30.0):\n        self.coordinator_id = coordinator_id\n        self.timeout = timeout\n        \n        self._transactions: Dict[str, DistributedTransaction] = {}\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n        self._running = False\n        self._cleanup_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None\n        \n        # Callbacks for participant communication\n        self._prepare_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._commit_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._abort_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self._running = \"\"\"Stop coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self._running = False\n        if self._cleanup_thread and self._cleanup_thread.is_alive():\n            self._cleanup_thread.join(timeout=1.0)\n    \n    def _cleanup_loop(self):\n        \"\"\"Background cleanup of expired transactions.\"\"\"\n        while self._running:\n            time.sleep(1.0)  # Short interval for testing\n            try:\n                self._cleanup_expired()\n            except:\n                pass\n    \n    def _cleanup_expired(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up expired transactions.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            now = time.time()\n            expired = [\n                txn_id for txn_id, txn in self._transactions.items()\n                if now - txn.start_time > self.timeout * 2\n                and        return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\n        elif txn.state == TransactionState.COMMITTING:\n            return self.commit_phase(txn_id)\n        elif txn.state == TransactionState.ABORTING:\n \"\"\"Append value to vector.\"\"\"\n        if self.size >= self.capacity:\n            self._grow()\n        \n        idx = self.size\n        if is_null:\n            self._set_null(idx)\n      byte_idx = idx // 8\n        bit_idx = idx % 8\n        self._null_bitmap[byte_idx] |= (1 << bit_idx)\n    \n    def is_null(self, idx: int) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if value at index is value at index.\"\"\"\n        if self.is_null(idx):\n            return None\n        return self._data[idx]\n    \n    def _grow(self):\n        \"\"\"Grow storage capacity.\"\"\"\n <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "I'll implement **Task 11: Schema migration system** - versioned schema changes with rollback support.\n\n<WriteFile>\n<fileName>schema_migration.py</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nSchema Migration System for KosDB\n\nVersioned schema changes with rollback support, dependency tracking,\nand transaction-safe migrations.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport re\nimport json\nimport time\nimport hashlib\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Callable, Tuple\nfrom enum import Enum, auto\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict\n\n\nclass MigrationStatus(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Status of a migration.\"\"\"\n    PENDING = auto()\n    APPLIED = auto()\n    ROLLED_BACK = auto()\n    FAILED = auto()\n\n\nclass MigrationType(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Type of migration operation.\"\"\"\n    CREATE_TABLE = auto()\n    DROP_TABLE = auto()\n    ALTER_TABLE = auto()\n    CREATE_INDEX = auto()\n    DROP_INDEX = auto()\n    RENAME_TABLE = auto()\n    CUSTOM = auto()\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass MigrationStep:\n    \"\"\"Single step in a migration.\"\"\"\n    step_id: str\n    operation: MigrationType\n    description: str\n    forward_sql: str\n    rollback_sql: str\n    dependencies: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    checksum: Optional[str] = None\n    \n    def __post_init__(self):\n        if self.checksum is None:\n            self.checksum = self._calculate_checksum()\n    \n    def _calculate_checksum(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Calculate checksum of migration content.\"\"\"\n        content = f\"{self.forward_sql}:{self.rollback_sql}\"\n        return hashlib.sha256(content.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]\n    \n    def verify_checksum(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Verify migration hasn't been tampered with.\"\"\"\n        return self.checksum == self._calculate_checksum()\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Migration:\n    \"\"\"A database migration.\"\"\"\n    migration_id: str\n    version: str\n    description: str\n    author: str\n    created_at: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    steps: List[MigrationStep] = field(default_factory=list)\n    status: MigrationStatus = MigrationStatus.PENDING\n    applied_at: Optional[float] = None\n    rolled_back_at: Optional[float] = None\n    execution_time_ms: Optional[float] = None\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Convert migration to dictionary.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            'migration_id': self.migration_id,\n            'version': self.version,\n            'description': self.description,\n            'author': self.author,\n            'created_at': self.created_at,\n            'steps': [\n                {\n                    'step_id': s.step_id,\n                    'operation': s.operation.name,\n                    'description': s.description,\n                    'dependencies': s.dependencies,\n                    'checksum': s.checksum\n                }\n                for s in self.steps\n            ],\n            'status': self.status.name,\n            'applied_at': self.applied_at,\n            'rolled_back_at': self.rolled_back_at,\n            'execution_time_ms': self.execution_time_ms\n        }\n\n\nclass SchemaVersion:\n    \"\"\"Manages schema versioning.\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, major: int = 0, minor: int = 0, patch: int = 0):\n        self.major = major\n        self.minor = minor\n        self.patch = patch\n    \n    @classmethod\n    def parse(cls, version_str: str) -> 'SchemaVersion':\n        \"\"\"Parse version string.\"\"\"\n        match = re.match(r'(\\d+)\\.(\\d+)\\.(\\d+)', version_str)\n        if not match:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid version: {version_str}\")\n        return cls(int(match.group(1)), int(match.group(2)), int(match.group(3)))\n    \n    def __str__(self) -> str:\n        return f\"{self.major}.{self.minor}.{self.patch}\"\n    \n    def __lt__(self, other: 'SchemaVersion') -> bool:\n        return (self.major, self.minor, self.patch) < (other.major, other.minor, other.patch)\n    \n    def __le__(self, other: 'SchemaVersion') -> bool:\n        return (self.major, self.minor, self.patch) <= (other.major, other.minor, other.patch)\n    \n    def __eq__(self, other: object) -> bool:\n        if not isinstance(other, SchemaVersion):\n            return False\n        return (self.major, self.minor, self.patch) == (other.major, other.minor, other.patch)\n\n\nclass MigrationExecutor:\n    \"\"\"\n    Executes migrations with transaction safety.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, db_connection: Any):\n        self.db = db_connection\n        self._pre_hooks: List[Callable] = []\n        self._post_hooks: List[Callable] = []\n        self._error_hooks: List[Callable] = []\n    \n    def add_pre_hook(self, hook: Callable[[MigrationStep], None]):\n        \"\"\"Add hook to run before each step.\"\"\"\n        self._pre_hooks.append(hook)\n    \n    def add_post_hook(self, hook: Callable[[MigrationStep, bool], None]):\n        \"\"\"Add hook to run after each step.\"\"\"\n        self._post_hooks.append(hook)\n    \n    def add_error_hook(self, hook: Callable[[MigrationStep, Exception], None]):\n        \"\"\"Add hook to run on step error.\"\"\"\n        self._error_hooks.append(hook)\n    \n    def execute_forward(self, migration: Migration) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute migration forward.\n        \n        Args:\n            migration: Migration to apply\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if successful\n        \"\"\"\n        start_time = time.time()\n        migration.status = MigrationStatus.PENDING\n        \n        try:\n            # Sort steps by dependencies\n            ordered_steps = self._topological_sort(migration.steps)\n            \n            for step in ordered_steps:\n                # Verify checksum\n                if not step.verify_checksum():\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Checksum mismatch for step {step.step_id}\")\n                \n                # Run pre-hooks\n                for hook in self._pre_hooks:\n                    hook(step)\n                \n                # Execute step\n                try:\n                    self._execute_sql(step.forward_sql)\n                    \n                    # Run post-hooks\n                    for hook in self._post_hooks:\n                        hook(step, True)\n                        \n                except Exception as e:\n                    for hook in self._error_hooks:\n                        hook(step, e)\n                    raise\n            \n            migration.status = MigrationStatus.APPLIED\n            migration.applied_at = time.time()\n            migration.execution_time_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000\n            return True\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            migration.status = MigrationStatus.FAILED\n            return False\n    \n    def execute_rollback(self, migration: Migration) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Rollback migration.\n        \n        Args:\n            migration: Migration to rollback\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if successful\n        \"\"\"\n        if migration.status != MigrationStatus.APPLIED:\n            return False\n        \n        try:\n            # Sort steps in reverse order for rollback\n            ordered_steps = self._topological_sort(migration.steps)\n            ordered_steps.reverse()\n            \n            for step in ordered_steps:\n                self._execute_sql(step.rollback_sql)\n            \n            migration.status = MigrationStatus.ROLLED_BACK\n            migration.rolled_back_at = time.time()\n            return True\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            return False\n    \n    def _topological_sort(self, steps: List[MigrationStep]) -> List[MigrationStep]:\n        \"\"\"Sort steps by dependencies.\"\"\"\n        step_map = {s.step_id: s for s in steps}\n        visited: set = set()\n        result: List[MigrationStep] = []\n        \n        def visit(step_id: str):\n            if step_id in visited:\n                return\n            visited.add(step_id)\n            step = step_map.get(step_id)\n            if step:\n                for dep in step.dependencies:\n                    visit(dep)\n                result.append(step)\n        \n        for step in steps:\n            visit(step.step_id)\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _execute_sql(self, sql: str):\n        \"\"\"Execute SQL statement.\"\"\"\n        # In real implementation, this would execute against database\n        if hasattr(self.db, 'execute'):\n            self.db.execute(sql)\n        elif hasattr(self.db, 'query'):\n            self.db.query(sql)\n\n\nclass MigrationHistory:\n    \"\"\"\n    Tracks migration history.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, storage_path: str = \".migrations\"):\n        self.storage_path = storage_path\n        self._migrations: Dict[str, Migration] = {}\n        self._ensure_storage()\n    \n    def _ensure_storage(self):\n        \"\"\"Ensure storage directory exists.\"\"\"\n        os.makedirs(self.storage_path, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    def record_migration(self, migration: Migration):\n        \"\"\"Record migration in history.\"\"\"\n        self._migrations[migration.migration_id] = migration\n        self._save_history()\n    \n    def get_migration(self, migration_id: str) -> Optional[Migration]:\n        \"\"\"Get migration by ID.\"\"\"\n        return self._migrations.get(migration_id)\n    \n    def get_applied_migrations(self) -> List[Migration]:\n        \"\"\"Get all applied migrations.\"\"\"\n        return [\n            m for m in self._migrations.values()\n            if m.status == MigrationStatus.APPLIED\n        ]\n    \n    def get_pending_migrations(self) -> List[Migration]:\n        \"\"\"Get all pending migrations.\"\"\"\n        return [\n            m for m in self._migrations.values()\n            if m.status == MigrationStatus.PENDING\n        ]\n    \n    def get_current_version(self) -> Optional[SchemaVersion]:\n        \"\"\"Get current schema version.\"\"\"\n        applied = self.get_applied_migrations()\n        if not applied:\n            return None\n        \n        versions = [SchemaVersion.parse(m.version) for m in applied]\n        return max(versions)\n    \n    def _save_history(self):\n        \"\"\"Save migration history to disk.\"\"\"\n        history_file = os.path.join(self.storage_path, \"history.json\")\n        data = {\n            mid: m.to_dict()\n            for mid, m in self._migrations.items()\n        }\n        with open(history_file, 'w') as f:\n            json.dump(data, f, indent=2)\n    \n    def load_history(self):\n        \"\"\"Load migration history from disk.\"\"\"\n        history_file = os.path.join(self.storage_path, \"history.json\")\n        if os.path.exists(history_file):\n            with open(history_file, 'r') as f:\n                data = json.load(f)\n            # Reconstruct migrations (simplified)\n <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "", "sessionId": 318, "rowId": 19, "timestamp": 1783710196.2365956, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "I'll implement **Task 12: Metrics and monitoring** - types.\"\"\"\n    COUNTER = auto()\n    GAUGE = auto()\n    HISTOGRAM = auto()\n    SUMMARY = auto()\n\n\nclass HealthStatus(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Health check status.\"\"\"\n    HEALTHY = \"healthy\"\n    DEGRADED = \"degraded\"\n    UNHEALTHY = \"unhealthy\"\n    UNKNOWN = \"unknown\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass MetricValue:\n    \"\"\"Single metric value with timestamp.\"\"\"\n    value: float\n    timestamp: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    labels: Dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n\nclass Metric:\n    \"\"\"\n    Base metric class.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, name: str, metric_type: MetricType,\n                 description: str = \"\", labels: Optional[List[str]] = None):\n        self.name = name\n        self.metric_type = metric_type\n        self.description = description\n        self.label_names = labels or []\n        self._values: Dict[str, MetricValue] = {}\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n    \n    def _label_key(self, labels: Dict[str, str]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate key from labels.\"\"\"\n        if not labels:\n            return \"__default__\"\n        return \":\".join(f\"{k}={v}\" for k, v in sorted(labels.items()))\n    \n    def inc(self, value: float = 1.0, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Increment counter metric.\"\"\"\n        if self.metric_type != MetricType.COUNTER:\n            raise TypeError(\"inc() only valid for counters\")\n        \n        key = self._label_key(labels)\n        with self._lock:\n            if key in self._values:\n                self._values[key].value += value\n            else:\n                self._values[key] = MetricValue(value, labels=labels or {})\n    \n    def set(self, value: float, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Set gauge metric value.\"\"\"\n        if self.metric_type not in (MetricType.GAUGE, MetricType.COUNTER):\n            raise TypeError(\"set() only valid for gauges and counters\")\n        \n        key = self._label_key(labels)\n        with self._lock:\n            self._values[key] = MetricValue(value, labels=labels or {})\n    \n    def observe(self, value: float, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Observe value for histogram/summary.\"\"\"\n        if self.metric_type not in (MetricType.HISTOGRAM, MetricType.SUMMARY):\n            raise TypeError(\"observe() only valid for histograms and summaries\")\n        \n        key = self._label_key(labels)\n        with self._lock:\n            if key not in self._values:\n                self._values[key] = MetricValue(0.0, labels=labels or {})\n                self._values[key]._observations: deque = deque(maxlen=1000)\n            \n            self._values[key]._observations.append(value)\n    \n    def get_value(self, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None) -> Optional[float]:\n        \"\"\"Get current value.\"\"\"\n        key = self._label_key(labels)\n        with self._lock:\n            val = self._values.get(key)\n            return val.value if val else None\n    \n    def get_all_values(self) -> Dict[str, MetricValue]:\n        \"\"\"Get all labeled values.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return dict(self._values)\n    \n    def to_prometheus(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Export in Prometheus format.\"\"\"\n        lines = []\n        \n        # Type annotation\n        type_map = {\n            MetricType.COUNTER: \"counter\",\n            MetricType.GAUGE: \"gauge\",\n            MetricType.HISTOGRAM: \"histogram\",\n            MetricType.SUMMARY: \"summary\"\n        }\n        \n        lines.append(f\"# HELP {self.name} {self.description}\")\n        lines.append(f\"# TYPE {self.name} {type_map[self.metric_type]}\")\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            for key, val in self._values.items():\n                label_str = \"\"\n                if   lines.append(f\"{self.name}{label_str} {val.value}\")\n        \n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n    \n    def clear(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear all values.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            self._values.clear()\n\n\nclass Histogram(Metric):\n    \"\"\"\n    Histogram metric with configurable buckets.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    DEFAULT_BUCKETS = [.005, .01, .025, .05, .075, .1, .25,              labels: Optional[List[str]] = None):\n        super().__init__(name, MetricType.HISTOGRAM, description, labels)\n        self.buckets = sorted(buckets or self.DEFAULT_BUCKETS)\n self._bucket_counts[key]['count'] += 1\n    \n    def to_prometheus(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Export histogram in Prometheus format.\"\"\"\n        lines = []\n        lines.append(f\"# HELP product similarity\n    MANHATTAN = auto()   # L1 distance\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass VectorDocument:\n    \"\"\"A document with vector embedding.\"\"\"\n    doc_id: str\n    vector: List[float]\n    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    created_at: float = field(default_factory=lambda: __import__('time').time())\n    \n    def __post_init__(self):\n        # Normalize vector for cosine similarity\n        self._norm = math.sqrt(sum(x * x for x in self.vector))\n    \n    def normalize(self) -> List[float]:\n        \"\"\"Get normalized vector.\"\"\"\n        if self._norm == 0:\n            return self.vector\n        return [x / self._norm for x in self.vector]\n\n\nclass VectorIndex:\n    \"\"\"\n    In-memory vector index for similarity search.\n    Supports self.metric = metric\n        self._documents: Dict[str, VectorDocument] = {}\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n        \n        # For IVF (Inverted File Index)\n        self._n_clusters = 0\n \"\"\"\n        Search for k nearest neighbors.\n        \n        Args:\n            query_vector: Query embedding\n            k: Number of results\n            filter_fn: Optional filter function\n        \n        Returns:\n            List of (doc_id, score) tuples, sorted by score\n        \"\"\"\n        if len(query_vector) != self.dimension:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Expected def _brute_force_search(self, query_vector: List[float], k: int,\n                           filter_fn: Optional[Callable] = None) -> List[Tuple[str, float]]:\n        \"\"\"Brute force search over all documents.\"\"\"\n        scores = []\n        \n        for doc_id, doc in self._documents.items():\n            if filter_fn and not filter_fn(doc):\n                continue\n            \n            score = self._compute_similarity(query_vector, doc.vector)\n            scores.append((doc_id, score))\n        \n        # Return top k\n        scores.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n        return scores[:k]\n    \n    def _ivf_search(self, query_vector: List[float], k: int,\n                   filter_fn: Optional[Callable] = None) -> List[Tuple[str, float]]:\n        \"\"\"Search using Inverted File Index.\"\"\"\n        # Find nearest centroids\n        centroid_scores = [\n            (i, self._compute_similarity(query_vector, centroid))\n            for i, centroid in enumerate(self._centroids)\n        ]\n        centroid_scores.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n        \n        # Search top n_probe clusters\n        n_probe = min(3, self._n_clusters)\n        candidates = []\n        \n        for cluster_id, _ in centroid_scores[:n_probe]:\n            for doc_id in self._inverted_lists[cluster_id]:\n                doc = self._documents.get(doc_id)\n                if doc and (not filter_fn or filter_fn(doc)):\n                    score = self._compute_similarity(query_vector, doc.vector)\n                    candidates.append((doc_id, score))\n        \n        # Return top k\n        candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n        return candidates[:k]\n    \n    def _compute_similarity(self, v1: List[float], v2: List[float]) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Compute similarity between two vectors.\"\"\"\n        if self.metric == DistanceMetric.COSINE:\n            return self._cosine_similarity(v1, v2)\n        elif self.metric == DistanceMetric.EUCLIDEAN:\n            return -self._euclidean_distance(v1, v2)  # Negative for sorting\n        elif self.metric == DistanceMetric.DOT_PRODUCT:\n            return sum(a * b for a, b in zip(v1, v2))\n        elif self.metric == DistanceMetric.MANHATTAN:\n            return -sum(abs(a - b) for a, b in zip(v1, v2))\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown metric: {self.metric}\")\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def _cosine_similarity(v1: List[float], v2: List[float]) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Compute cosine similarity.\"\"\"\n        dot = sum(a * b for a, b in zip(v1, v2))\n        norm1 = math.sqrt(sum(a * a for a in v1))\n        norm2 = math.sqrt(sum(b * b for b in v2))\n        \n        if norm1 == 0 or norm2 == 0:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        return dot / (norm1 * norm2)\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def _euclidean_distance(v1: List[float], v2: List[float]) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Compute Euclidean distance.\"\"\"\n        return math.sqrt(sum((a - b) ** 2 for a, b in zip(v1, v2)))\n    \n    def train_ivf(self, n_clusters: int = 10):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train IVF index using k-means clustering.\n        \n        Args:\n            n_clusters: Number of clusters\n        \"\"\"\n        if len(self._documents) < n_clusters:\n            return  # Not enough documents\n        \n        with self._lock:\n Build inverted lists\n            self._inverted_lists.clear()\n            for doc_id, doc in self._documents.items():\n                cluster_id = self._assign_to_cluster(doc.vector)\n                self._inverted_lists[cluster_id].append(doc_id)\n            \n            self._is_trained = True\n    \n    def _kmeans(self, vectors: List[List[float]], k: int, \n                max_iters: int = 10) -> List[List[float]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Simple k-means clustering.\n        \n        Args:\n            vectors: List of vectors\n            k: Number of clusters\n            max_iters: Maximum iterations\n        \n        Returns:\n            Cluster centroids\n        \"\"\"\n        if not vectors:\n            return []\n        \n        # Random initialization\n        centroids = random.sample(vectors, k)\n        \n        for _ in range(max_iters):\n            # Assign to clusters\n            clusters: Dict[int, List[List[float]]] = defaultdict(list)\n            for v in vectors:\n                distances = [\n                    self._euclidean_distance(v, c) \n                    for c in centroids\n                ]\n                cluster_id = distances.index(min(distances))\n                clusters[cluster_id].append(v)\n            \n            # Update centroids\n            new_centroids = []\n            for i in range(k):\n                if i in clusters and clusters[i]:\n                    # Compute mean\n                    mean = [\n                        sum(v[j] for v in clusters[i]) / len(clusters[i])\n                        for j in range(self.dimension)\n                    ]\n                    new_centroids.append(mean)\n                else:\n                    new_centroids.append(centroids[i])\n            \n            centroids = new_centroids\n        \n        return centroids\n    \n    def _assign_to_cluster(self, vector: List[float]) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Assign vector to nearest cluster.\"\"\"\n        distances = [\n            self._euclidean_distance(vector, c)\n            for c in self._centroids\n        ]\n        return distances.index(min(distances))\n    \n    def get_stats(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get index statistics.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return {\n                'dimension': self.dimension,\n                'metric': self.metric.name,\n                'num_documents': len(self._documents),\n                'num_clusters': self._n_clusters,\n                'is_trained': self._is_trained\n            }\n\n\nclass self._lock = threading.RLock()\n    \n    def create_index(self, name: str, dimension: int,\n                     metric: DistanceMetric = DistanceMetric.COSINE) -> VectorIndex:\n        \"\"\"\n        Create new vector index.\n        \n        Args:\n            name: Index name\n            dimension: Vector dimension\n            metric: Distance metric\n        \n        Returns:\n            Created index\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            if name in self._indexes:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Index {name} already exists\")\n            \n            index = VectorIndex(dimension, metric)\n            self._indexes[name] = index\n            return index\n    \n    def get_index(self, name: str) -> Optional[VectorIndex]:\n        \"\"\"Get index by name.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return self._indexes.get(name)\n    \n    def delete_index(self, name: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Delete index.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            if name not in self._indexes:\n                return False\n            del self._indexes[name]\n            return True\n    \n    def list_indexes(self) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"List all index names.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return list(self._indexes.keys())\n    \n    def search(self, index_name: str, query_vector: List[float],\n               k: int = 10, **kwargs) -> List[Tuple[str, float]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Search index.\n        \n        Args:\n            index_name: Index to search\n            query_vector: Query embedding\n            k: Number of results\n            **kwargs: Additional search parameters\n        \n        Returns:\n            Search results\n        \"\"\"\n        index = self.get_index(index_name)\n        if not index:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Index {index_name} not found\")\n        \n        return index.search(query_vector, k, **kwargs)\n    \n    def hybrid_search(self, index_name: str, query_vector: List[float],\n                     keyword_filter: Optional[str] = None,\n                     k: int = 10) -> List[Tuple[str, float, Dict[str, Any]]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Hybrid search combining vector similarity with keyword filtering.\n        \n        Args:\n            index_name: Index to search\n            query_vector: Query embedding\n            keyword_filter: Optional keyword to filter results\n            k: Number of results\n        \n        Returns:\n            Results with metadata\n        \"\"\"\n        index = self.get_index(index_name)\n        if not index:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Index {index_name} not found\")\n        \n        # Create filter function\n        filter_fn = None\n        if keyword_filter:\n            def filter_fn(doc):\n                text = json.dumps(doc.metadata).lower()\n                return keyword_filter.lower() in text\n        \n        results = index.search(query_vector, k * 2, filter_fn=filter_fn)\n        \n        # Enrich with metadata\n        enriched = []\n        for doc_id, score in results[:k]:\n            doc = index._documents.get(doc_id)\n            if doc:\n                enriched.append((doc_id, score, doc.metadata))\n        \n        return enriched\n\n\nclass EmbeddingGenerator:\n    \"\"\"\n    Interface for generating embeddings from text.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, dimension: int = 384):\n        self.dimension = dimension\n    \n    def encode(self, text: str) -> List[float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate embedding for text.\n        \n        Args:\n            text: Input text\n        \n        Returns:\n            Embedding vector\n        \"\"\"\n        # Simple hash-based embedding for demo\n        # In production, use sentence-transformers or similar\n        random.seed(hash(text) % (2**32))\n        return [random.gauss(0, 1) for _ in range(self.dimension)]\n    \n    def encode_batch(self, texts: List[str]) -> List[List[float]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate embeddings for multiple texts.\n        \n        Args:\n            texts: List of texts\n        \n        Returns:\n            List of embeddings\n        \"\"\"\n        return [self.encode(t) for t in texts]\n\n\nclass SemanticSearcher:\n    \"\"\"\n    High-level semantic search interface.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, engine: Optional[VectorSearchEngine] = None,\n                 embedding_gen: Optional[EmbeddingGenerator] = None):\n        self.engine = engine or VectorSearchEngine()\n        self.embedding_gen = embedding_gen or EmbeddingGenerator()\n    \n    def index_document(self, index_name: str, doc_id: str, \n                       text: str, metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):\n        \"\"\"\n        Index document with text content.\n        \n        Args:\n            index_name: Index name\n            doc_id: Document ID\n            text: Document text\n            metadata: Optional metadata\n        \"\"\"\n        index = self.engine.get_index(index_name)\n        if not index:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Index {index_name} not found\")\n        \n        embedding = self.embedding_gen.encode(text)\n        \n        meta = metadata or {}\n        meta['text'] = text  # Store original text\n        \n        index.add(doc_id, embedding, meta)\n    \n    def search(self, index_name: str, query: str, k: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Semantic search.\n        \n        Args:\n            index_name: Index name\n            query: Search query\n            k: Number of results\n        \n        Returns:\n            Search results with text and scores\n        \"\"\"\n        query_embedding = self.embedding_gen.encode(query)\n        \n        results = self.engine.hybrid_search(\n            index_name, \n            query_embedding,\n            k=k\n        )\n        \n        return [\n            {\n                'doc_id': doc_id,\n                'score': score,\n                'metadata': metadata\n            }\n            for doc_id, score, metadata in results\n        ]\n\n\n# Utility functions\ndef normalize_vector(vector: List[float]) -> List[float]:\n    \"\"\"Normalize vector to unit length.\"\"\"\n    norm = math.sqrt(sum(x * x for x in vector))\n    if norm == 0:\n        return vector\n    return [x / norm for x in vector]\n\n\ndef cosine_similarity(v1: List[float], v2: List[float]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"Compute cosine similarity between two vectors.\"\"\"\n    dot = sum(a * b for a, b in zip(v1, v2))\n    norm1 = math.sqrt(sum(a * a for a in v1))\n    norm2 = math.sqrt(sum(b * b for b in v2))\n    \n    if norm1 == 0 or norm2 == 0:\n        return 0.0\n    \n    return dot / (norm1 * norm2)\n\n\ndef euclidean_distance(v1: List[float], v2: List[float]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"Compute Euclidean distance.\"\"\"\n    return math.sqrt(sum((a - b) ** 2 for a, b in zip(v1, v2)))\n\n\ndef dot_product(v1: List[float], v2: List[float]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"Compute dot product.\"\"\"\n    return sum(a * b for a, b in zip(v1, v2))\n</contentOfFile>\n</WriteFile>", "sessionId": 318, "rowId": 20, "timestamp": 1783710254.1062677, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 45649, "response_tokens": 3872} -->
